This place was wonderful to store our items. We were in the second floor and we were happy with the location of the storage. There is an elevator for the heavier items so you don't have to lug them up. The guys that work there were also very nice and always available when we had a question. <user_id>100505829568448093460< /user_id><name>Christopher Maue< /name><date>1372708091032< /date><Rate>3<//Rate>< review>
I *would* have rated this storage place as *excellent* had the following not occurred:

After paying for the insurance provided by A-1 for many months, i gave them my paperwork for my own personal renters insurance. My monthly storage rental rate was supposed to be decreased by $10.... (which i was paying twice that amount for my renters insurance)....

Well *2 days!!!* after they accepted my renters insurance policy, i get a letter stating that "due to normal operating costs' or something similar, that they are "forced" to increase the rental fees when necessary (and the letter states this can happen twice a year)....

I have had rental units for over 10 years, and i know that sometimes rates do fluctuate... however, i hadn't even had my unit 1 year, and my bill was increasing...

I just think it was a little too "coincidental" that the "necessary increase" just happened to be the same $10 amt. that i was supposed to be saving from my renters insurance....  If my storage unit rental rate is going to be increasing 2 times a year, then i will most definitely be shopping for a new location pronto.<//review>

Quality Excellent

If you are in the market to upgrade your car audio system it would be in your best interest to swing by Pacific Stereo before you go anywhere else! Aside from their knowledgable staff, reasonable prices and huge inventory these guys have the absolute BEST customer service your money can buy hands down!!! Im a first time customer and came in for a car alarm, new head unit, small amp and an 8inch sub with a custom box for my Chevy Colorado at the Riverside location on the corner of Tyler and Indiana just south of the mall. The guys at this location (namely Jose) went above and beyond the call of duty to ensure my satisfaction with the services they performed and I COULD NOT be HAPPIER. Jose even showed some Christmas Spirit and hooked me up with brand new out of the box Alpine speakers to replace the stock ones in the doors at NO ADDITIONAL CHARGE!!! Who does that anymore? Sure I spent more than a couple of hours at the shop (which is why I think that Christmas Spirit came out) but hey, you cant rush the quality you get here or beat their customer satisfaction guarantee. Besides all that this place is a family friendly business with a comfortable lounge area where you and the kids can sit and watch all the sponge bob and power rangers you want on netflix or shop around in the neighboring businesses a stones throw away. I highly recommend Pacific Stereo to everyone looking to put a system in their ride and strongly urge you to ask for Jose. This guy hooked me up and I know he'll hook you up too! Thank you so much Jose and the whole Pacific Stereo team! Have a very Merry Christmas and God bless you all.</Text>

<username>F1 Racer</username><pictures>None</pictures><Rate>5</Rate><Review>This is a relatively laid back outfit, the largest car stereo shop I've come across anywhere. I dealt with Chris, who manages this local shop. What stood out for me compared to other shops I've tried around SoCal is that there's no high-pressure sales tactics, prices are reasonable, and the shop looks well run and organized. ( DO you know how hard it is to just find a shop with these attributes around SoCal?? not easy). Most other shops will try and up sell you unnecessarily, play games with installation and parts charges(inflated costs), and charge as much as they can get, kinda like how it is buying a car from a dealership, and we all know how much we love those experiences. The purchase process went smoothly. Chris was accommodating on the installation and got it done quickly. Now comes the real reason why I gave this outfit a five star. The installation was rushed a bit due to time constraints on my part, as a result, it also caused some errors to occur during installation. Both front woofer were damaged. The rubber surround edge were broken probably when the installer was securing the speaker. Now I found this out a week later after hearing some rattling, and wanted to install some dynamat. I called Chris and texted him a picture of each speaker, and discussed the issue. Chris was very responsive, and took care of the issue the very next day. He replaced them with new woofers. What's important about customer service isn't when everything goes well, it's when things don't go as planned. While my purchase experience didn't go perfectly smooth, but I leaned something about how Pacific stereo does business, their customer service focus, business integrity, and ethics. JFK puts it best " don't let an error become a mistake by refusing to fix it". More importantly, it tells me that this outfit is batting for the long game, and that is a good thing for the community it serves. Bravo.< /Review><gmapID>0x80dcb0b3557c23c9:0x68125917e142e62b<//gmapID>< time>

<user>108129027111070929454</user>< Text>
Beautiful location! Can't beat the views! The trail down to the beach is unpaved with many steps (not handicapped accessable), no railings, be careful with small children and elderly. Great place to hang out for the day, bring a lunch and maybe beach umbrella as there is no shade. Bathrooms are in the parking lot area and so are garbages. Clean up after yourselves to keep the beach trash free! Go during low tide to check out the tide pools, we saw a variety of sea life including two giant star fish!<//Text>

< Text>
Have been buying little replacement parts from this shop for years.  Great local business that always has just the right part at just the right time.  Owner Fred is a wealth of knowledge about all things appliance related.  I have long recommended this place for advice and replacement parts, and I have made sent numerous family and friends to Miracle Appliance.

Today I had a very odd experience with the owner however.  Long story short, I ended up purchasing a $170 ice maker part that ended up not solving my issue.  I explained that after swapping this part into my fridge, the errors persisted and I called a repair company to diagnose and fix. A different fix was required, so the ice maker that I purchased was not needed.

Though there are signs clearly posted in the business and on the receipts stating all sales are final/no returns, I figured that I'd at least ask if something could be done.  When I came into the store, Fred immediately started the return process , took my card and provided a receipt without me actually asking to do a return.  Great so far, but when he returned from the credit card machine, he chastised me about using him as a spare parts depot to diagnose my problem at his expense.  He asked for my receipt, which I had left at home, and when I told him as much, he said I didn't bring it because it has the no returns/refunds language displayed.  His typically jovial demeanor changed on a dime and he basically said that he couldn't take a chance selling me any parts in the future because he couldn't risk me trying to return them.  When I tried to engage him in a discussion to indicate that if he didn't want to take the return, and and I'd be OK with that, he asked me to leave the store so he could help the next customers in line.

To Fred, the owner:  this is crazy!  Here are some things you could have done to handle the situation better:

1) Just say no to returns -- You clearly indicate all sales are final, and that's fine, no dispute here.  Totally acceptable policy, but if you decide to bend your policy for a given customer, no need for the accusatory argument about being used as a test parts depot.  Your comment about me being old enough to know that asking for a return was rude, as was your comment about $170 being significant to you but implying it was not significant to me.

2) Restocking fees may apply -- Though the part I initially purchased was in a box, and had no documentation, plastic wrapping etc. and could easily have been an open-box/returned part, I assumed it was new from the factory.  You mentioned that you could no longer sell this part as new, and I get that, but how about you ask for a reasonable restocking fee that allows you resell the part as used without taking a gross margin hit?  Take 15 minutes, do a continuity check and get the part back on the shelf. Seems like common sense.

3) You're cut off -- I felt like I was in that Seinfeld episode with the restaurateur that sells soup, you know the one.  Basically telling me to leave your store and that you wouldn't sell me any other parts because I might try to return them is outrageous.  Having a conversation rather than dismissing me from your store would have gone a long way, and would likely have resulted in me continuing to make purchases from your business and continuing to make recommendations to my network.

I know how hard you work in your store, and your sage advice has saved me countless thousands of dollars in repair costs in the past, but this type of interaction is really unacceptable.  In COVID times I've tried to spend my money with local businesses rather than the online retailers, but banning me from your store means more business for Amazon.  Would love to continue the discussion if you care to discuss.</Text>

< Review>
Where do I even begin?
I've heard stories about this little hole in the wall store that's packed wall to wall floor to ceiling with parts in no obvious order.  Barely enough room to slide sideways down the aisles and this genius of a man who always knows what part you need and where its at.
Both my kids are down with the flu, doing non stop loads of laundry (clothes, towels, and bedding) to try and keep my wife and I from getting it and prevent relapse of the kids.  The dryer stops drying.
My first instinct is look it up online.  I do a search for my model and symptom.  Everything I read says replace the thermostat, I get the part number and call the only place I know of that should have the part.
Fred answers the phone and ever so kindly asks me to hold please.  (Not a real "hold", he just set the phone down and finished helping the customer in front of him while I listened on the phone.)
He came back to me and asked how he could help.  I asked him if he had the part i needed, told him the model number of my dryer and the part number i was needing.
Fred's response "Why do you think you need that part?", "What is the issue you are having?".
I explain and he says "You don't need that part", "Why don't you remove parts x,y, & z and bring them in to me and I'll test them."
"and you better hurry, i close at 1pm".  It was about 11:45 so I quickly tore the machine apart and removed every part in the area of the thermostat that I could easily remove (because I couldn't remember the specific parts he told me).
I rushed over to the store and found exactly what I've heard about it.
I waited for Fred to finish with the customer ahead of me and then it was my turn.
He greeted me so incredably kindly and I laid all my parts on the counter.  I told him I had just called about the Dryer and I hoped these were all the parts he told me to bring.  He confirmed I brought everything.  He took out a voltmeter and proceeded to explain to me what value each should show as he tested and showed me each one.  There was one part that was slightly off, the rest read the correct readings.
He walked back to a shelf and came back with a small bag with two parts in it.
He took them out and put a little red marker mark on each.
He handed me the bag and said "This is your problem, take these and put them in and if it works you owe me $30".
I tried to argue "How about I give you the $30 and if it doesn't work I'll come back." I told him that I couldn't be back before 1pm when he closed.  Fred would not have it and told me come back after the weekend then scooted me out the door.
I went home installed the parts, put it all back together and low and behold it worked!
I will be returning tomorrow (Monday) to pay Fred the $30 I owe him and thank him profusely.
I told my wife the story of the nicest, kindest, most customer oriented man I've ever met in my life and I HAD to write this review.
Fred is AMAZING, One of a Kind!< /Review>

Got off work at 5pm drove home, removed the fan and board in 15min it was 5:35pm and I called and he picked up I told him that I need 2 parts he said come on down, i'll be here. The moment I came in I saw Fred and introduced myself and it was 5:45pm (he closes at 5:30pm) I told him of my problem and he already had the parts in-front of him and began dissecting my old fan and removed the thermostat sensor and began plugging it into the new fan. Being a do-it-yourself kind of guy I figured he just saved me $30 because the evap fan with thermostat was $110 (search from earlier in the day). We began to talk and he saw my motherboard and I told him I needed to get this too since most of the boards online mention to replace this as-well since the fan went out. Anyhow Fred inspects and tells me this board is in good shape and show'd me the resistor and etc that usually go bad. Then he tells me  I didn't need to buy the board  and spend $200 and said"are you sure" and he says "trust me why spend the money." < text>
This was my first visit to a Flights restaurant and I thought the concept was really fun. Everything they serve is a "flight" with multiple variations of the same dish or drink - perfect for the person who has trouble deciding what they want. For example, the flight of mac n' cheese came with three mini skillets of different types of mac n' cheese to try. The "flight attendants" (aka servers) thing was kind of corny, but I loved that there was a button that let you call if you needed something. I wasn't blown away by the food overall but they get points for the concept.<//text>

< Review>
Food and service are all excellent here. Prices are reasonable too. You can choose standard tables or the lounge.
Food and beer is delivered in 3s, which is the theme here. I suggest you do a family style and share you various 3-combos. We tend to mix the various appetizers and entrees together and let food come as it is ready. The flavors are really good and often very different from other restaurants. The 3 smallish items per serving means you get to experiment with things you might not have tried. This is now our favorite family restaurant for everything above and the excellent wait/bar staff.
This is so interesting to eat at I strongly urge you to try it< /Review>

<user_name>Sam Sedighian< /user_name><rate>3</rate><Gmap_id>0x808e35ee4b03a399:0x3ded25c54efac275< /Gmap_id><date>1557940365697< /date></record></dataset><record>
<user>115254748586261217847</user>< user_name>
Nancy Lee<//user_name>
<Time>1516124313717<//Time><rating>5</rating>< Review>
I was excited to try this place! The idea of combining tapas/flights seemed perfect for a happy hour with a friend. Plus during actual happy hour it's 25% off the menu!

VIBE: located in beautiful downtown Campbell! Decent sized place with a bar and good amount of tables

SERVICE: how cute that all the waiters are like "flight attendants"! They also give you a card to flip up at the table when you need service or when you're "ready for take off". Kinda cheesy but convenient!

FOOD: if you check in on Yelp you get a free glass of champagne!

Tropical cocktails- pina colada, strawberry daiquiri and mai tai. Don't let their tiny size fool you, these were STRONG.

French fries- truffle, garlic and sweet potato each with their own dipping sauces. My favorite dip was with the sweet potato!

Mac n Cheese- classic, truffle, and bacon/jalape√±o. Surprisingly I preferred the bacon over the truffle which wasn't that flavorful.

BBQ Sliders- These were difficult to share since we had to cut these tiny messy sliders in half. But I thought they paired well with the other flights

Overall our happy hour was enjoyable, and our server didn't try to rush us to finish even though the restaurant was getting pretty crowded as it got closer to peak dinner time. I think its only worth it to come here for happy hour because for a couple of flights it added to be pretty pricy (~$60 after tip) and I didn't think the food was that unique, just insta-worthy presentation.< /Review>

Has a great time at Flights.  Cute aviation uniforms and vernacular, family style comfort food.  Here all the dishes and drinks come by default in flights of three variations.  Staff was super helpful and nice. The portions were not skimpy and the food was good.  Drinks good too, but given the local bounty, I do think there was room for improvement there. < text>
Flights is not what it used to be, at least not in Los Gatos. Once, they boasted a large menu of innovative dishes, each offered in a trio (a "flight") featuring variations on a theme. Each dish was well-prepared and delicious.  Unfortunately, times change.

Flights had changed hands, and the menu, and food quality, have changed with it.  The new menu still has a few flights, but the bulk of the food is offered in "bites".  This would be fine if the quality had been maintained.  Unfortunately, the new menu is loaded with food that is bland and uninspired. The "Korean" Buffalo Chicken looked fancy on the plate, but it tasted like fried chicken nuggets drizzled in Frank's Red Hot sauce. It was mostly heat and little flavor. The sliders also looked great, but tasted rather plain, even the Chipotle Beef slider, which featured avocado and corn etole. The biggest letdown was the "Reverse Cheesecake" flight that we ordered for dessert. Essentially cheesecake in three jars, each topped with different toppings. The most flavorful part of the entire flight was the Oreo crumble on the chocolate entry.  The strawberry topping was merely adequate, and the mango topping was clearly fermented. The cheesecake itself was loose and bland.

On the plus side, the wait staff was very friendly.  Still, we likely won't be back anytime soon.< /text>

<Rating>1<//Rating><text>After having a sub-par experience at the Flights location in Campbell, I was hopeful that the Los Gatos location may redeem this place. I went for a birthday party with a group of girls and somehow the experience was even worse. The food was not good at all (the grilled cheese was especially disappointing- how can you mess that up so bad?), but the service was possibly the worst I've ever experienced at a restaurant. The restaurant anyway expects you to press a button to receive service which is strange to me, but we had to press the buttons over and over to get someone to come wait on our table. We ran out of water multiple times and couldn't get anyone to bring more, we waited a very long time to have someone bring a to-go box, they didn't bus our table until we left basically so as we chatted, there was just mess everywhere, and several dishes came out cold. To top it all off, the event planner told the person who planned the night that we wouldn't need to pay a minimum when she was making the reservation, yet when the bill came, there was a minimum fee added to the bill. When we approached them, they said it's non-negotiable which was frustrating enough, but they also never pro-actively presented the opportunity to us to actually order more food/dessert to meet it so we essentially were all forced to split an extra $250 that the restaurant just pocketed since we didn't know about this minimum until we were all ready to leave. To finish out the series of unfortunate events, the waitress came up to us rudely at 9:30 to tell us we needed to leave because the restaurant had been closed for 30 minutes (again, they hadn't even bussed our table so they didn't seem to be in much of a hurry and there are much nicer ways to do this). <rating>5</rating>< date>

< review>
Flights in Los Gatos is far superior to the Campbell location. As I have gone to both a number of times here are my comparisions.
Both restaurants: The whole concept of Flights is very cute and a food lover's dream. The decor is air travel, the servers dress like flight attendants, and there is a call button on your table airplane style. Most of the food/drinks are served in "flights" of 3, tapas style. That isnt to say you have to share and some things, like salads and flatbreads are served in normal portions.
Campbell: Limited seating and food seems to be prepared more hastily than Los Gatos. (I'll go into more detail in my review of the campbell location).
Los Gatos: Ample indoor and outdoor seating, plus bar seating. I've only visited this location during weekday lunch hours and it is never busy, though I'm not sure why. There is also ample parking between their own small lot and the large shared lot behind the restaurant.
Food: Honestly everything I've tried has been good but I most highly recommend the ceviche, steak tacos, and Stix (way bigger than they look on the menu). I don't eat gluten or dairy and there are tons of options for me. Only thing I've tried that I would probably not order again is the sliders, they do have GF buns but they are pretty dry and the burgers aren't anything exciting.

Overall, I highly recommend Flights Los Gatos for business, groups of friends or families. It is also sure to impress out of town guests.< /review>

<Rating>3< /Rating>< Text>
In A Nutshell:

-Flights really took off w/ a great idea.
-They serve everything, "flight" style, think 3's.
-With that being said, I was slightly disappointed w/ the service.
-I am not sure the "team" concept works very well when if your plates stack up and each team member walks by w/ out clearing the table, possibly thinking the next team member "might do it".
-As a customer you probably shouldn't have to ask, especially at this place when you know things are going to stack up pretty fast.
-The food itself was good, but can improve.
-The waffles could be warmer and less soggy.
-The bacon and beer flight took too long to come out and the bacon soaks up the beer making it soggy.
-I really liked the eggs benedict flight and would order again.

Overall, I hate writing reviews about service, but for now this place gets 3 stars.  It can easily improve and I will give it another shot.<//Text>

Flights has a fun and well executed theme and concept.  The decor is themed to the classic era of commercial aviation.  And everything on the menu comes in flights of three variations on an idea, all distinct and interesting, though you can opt to have only one or two variations if you prefer.  The ahi flight was good though not great.  I was extremely happy with all three variations on falafel, old fashioned cocktail, and cookies with ice cream.  You can probably find better single instances of anything on this menu, but if you crave diversity and variety in your dining, Flights is an excellent choice!</review>

We especially loved the plank filet (and the *amazing* duchesse potato), the duck breast, the mushroom risotto, and the roasted salmon.
